Reporting and enforcement
=========================

Learn about reporting content on YouTube, the actions our teams take when reviewing content, and what this means for you.

Report content
--------------

*   [Report inappropriate videos, channels, and other content on YouTube](/youtube/answer/2802027?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)
*   [Report a YouTube search prediction](/youtube/answer/7626105?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)
*   [Report policy-violative ads](/youtube/answer/10684207?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)
*   [About the YouTube Priority Flagger program](/youtube/answer/7554338?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)
*   [View your Reporting History](/youtube/answer/7687979?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)
*   [Other reporting options](/youtube/answer/2802057?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)
*   [Australian Online Safety Act and how to report online harm](/youtube/answer/14261249?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)

Learn about enforcements
------------------------

*   [How YouTube reviews content](/youtube/answer/13304829?hl=en&ref_topic=9387060)
*   [Community Guidelines strike basics on YouTube](/youtube/answer/2802032?hl=en&ref_topic=9387060)
*   [Age-restricted content](/youtube/answer/2802167?hl=en&ref_topic=9387060)
*   [Your YouTube content & Restricted Mode](/youtube/answer/7354993?hl=en&ref_topic=9387060)
*   [Watch age-restricted videos](/youtube/answer/10070779?hl=en&ref_topic=9387060)
*   [Videos locked as private](/youtube/answer/7300965?hl=en&ref_topic=9387060)
*   [Channel or account terminations](/youtube/answer/2802168?hl=en&ref_topic=9387060)
*   [Limited features for certain videos](/youtube/answer/7458465?hl=en&ref_topic=9387060)
*   [Strikes FAQ](/youtube/answer/9235777?hl=en&ref_topic=9387060)

Manage enforcements
-------------------

*   [Respond to enforcements](/youtube/answer/13304628?hl=en&ref_topic=9387083)
*   [Appeal a Community Guidelines strike or video removal](/youtube/answer/185111?hl=en&ref_topic=9387083)
*   [Age-restrict your own video on YouTube](/youtube/answer/2950063?hl=en&ref_topic=9387083)
*   [Troubleshoot video takedowns](/youtube/answer/6395024?hl=en&ref_topic=9387083)
